NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

A. Balakumar a male child born to Thiru K. Arumugam on 19th October 1987, residing at No.45, Mariamman Kovil 
Street, Kurinji Nagar, Ramapuram Post, Cuddalore-607 003, has been living as a female. She has been granded an Identity Card 
No.CUD/053/2019 issued by the Tamil Nadu Third Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department this, I may be 
treated as female and shall henceforth be known as A. LAKSHANYA
Cuddalore, 
 
  A. ð£ô°ñ£˜ 
 
21st January 2020.

2nd Street, Natarajapuram, Pukkathurai, Kancheepuram-621 004, has been living as a female. She has been granted an
Identity Card No. KPM/104/2019 Issued by the Tamil Nadu Transgender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and MNP Department.
By this I may be treated as female and shall henceforth be known as A. RATHI
Kancheepuram, 
 
  A. PARTHIBAN  
21st January 2020.
